% List all emoji in HarfLaTeX
% Built from https://github.com/twitter/twemoji/blob/master/src/test/preview-svg.html

\RequirePackage{harfload}
\documentclass[a4paper,12pt]{article}
\usepackage{fontspec}
\usepackage{longtable}
\usepackage[luatex,margin=7mm]{geometry}
\usepackage{bxcoloremoji}
\usepackage{longtable}

\newcounter{myline}
\newcommand{\mylinecount}{\arabic{myline}\stepcounter{myline}}
\newcommand{\fontA}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf,+dist,+ccmp}]{Segoe UI Emoji}#1}}
\newcommand{\fontB}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf,+dist,+ccmp}]{Noto Color Emoji}#1}}
\newcommand{\fontC}[1]{{\coloremoji*{#1}}}
\newcommand{\fontD}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={mode=harf,+ccmp}]{Twemoji Mozilla}#1}}
\newcommand{\fontE}[1]{{\fontspec[Ligatures=Common,RawFeature={+ccmp}]{Symbola}#1}}
\newcommand{\fontF}[1]{{\fontspec[RawFeature={+ccmp}]{Segoe UI Symbol}#1}}

\setmainfont[RawFeature={mode=harf,+dist,+ccmp}]{Segoe UI Emoji}


\begin{document}
\noindent
List all emoji in Unicode 12.0 by HarfLaTeX\\
Built from https://github.com/twitter/twemoji/blob/master/src/test/preview-svg.html\\
BXcoloremoji: https://github.com/zr-tex8r/BXcoloremoji\\
Symbola: http://users.teilar.gr/%7Eg1951d/\\
Noto Color Emoji: https://github.com/googlefonts/noto-emoji/blob/master/NotoColorEmoji.ttf\\
Twitter Emoji in COLR/CPAL format: https://github.com/mozilla/twemoji-colr\\
Its newer version: https://github.com/KwanEsq/twemoji-colr/tree/v12\\
Twemoji in other formats: https://twitter.com/Informoji/status/835062741941485568\\
